0                                   8092              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                    8093              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8094              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8095              Ÿ  SPIE ROUTINE                                                       Ÿ
                                    8096              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8097              Ÿ  The SPIE routine handles three situations,                         Ÿ
                                    8098              Ÿ            a. DEBUG interrupts                                      Ÿ
                                    8099              Ÿ            b. expected interrupts                                   Ÿ
                                    8100              Ÿ            c. unexpected interrupts                                 Ÿ
                                    8101              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8102              Ÿ  DEBUG interrupts are handled by saving the current users state     Ÿ
                                    8103              Ÿ  information, stopping the user and starting the debugger user.     Ÿ
                                    8104              Ÿ  The debugger user allows the debuger to look at and change the     Ÿ
                                    8105              Ÿ  state information of the user being debugged.  All traps are       Ÿ
                                    8106              Ÿ  turned off during the debug break to avoid recursion.              Ÿ
                                    8107              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8108              Ÿ  Expected interrupts are handled by the spieroutine by branching    Ÿ
                                    8109              Ÿ  to the routine address saved in CVSPIEAD.  It is important to      Ÿ
                                    8110              Ÿ  note that CVSPIEAD is cleared by the dispatcher and is only        Ÿ
                                    8111              Ÿ  valid for sections of code that do not get dispatched.             Ÿ
                                    8112              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8113              Ÿ  Unexpected interrupts will generate a DEBUG break if a debugging   Ÿ
                                    8114              Ÿ  session is active, otherwise a failsoft bomb will occur.           Ÿ
                                    8115              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8116              Ÿ  The SPIE routine does not allow in general for recursion.  If      Ÿ
                                    8117              Ÿ  a program interrupt occurs while we are processing a previous      Ÿ
                                    8118              Ÿ  SPIE request (ie. we are in the middle of a trap pause),  then     Ÿ
                                    8119              Ÿ  we execute the second level SPIE routine below.  This in general   Ÿ
                                    8120              Ÿ  results in a failsoft bomb of the users session.                   Ÿ
                                    8121              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8122              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8123              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
00003A8                             8124              SPIEPROC LABEL ,                  SPECIAL ENTRY FOR SPIE
